===COMMIT START===
Commit Hash: bf3e0ea84ea533f5dfa92116de7271ea10510a6c
Author: dawid <dawid@dawid-laptop.Home>
Date: 2025-11-25 23:08:10 +0100
Subject: feat: add comprehensive documentation and complete settlement fails integration
Message Body:
This commit represents a major milestone in the Treasury API Interface project,
adding comprehensive narrative documentation for all components and completing
the Market Plumbing subsystem with full settlement fails integration.

Documentation Added (docs/):
- FISCAL_ANALYSIS.md: In-depth explanation of fiscal impulse, TGA dynamics,
  and government cash flow monitoring methodology
- FED_LIQUIDITY.md: Complete Net Liquidity framework, QE/QT regime detection,
  and SOFR-IORB spread analysis
- NY_FED_OPERATIONS.md: Repo/RRP operations, submission ratios, and money
  market reference rates explained with economic context
- SETTLEMENT_FAILS.md: Settlement fails as collateral scarcity indicator,
  primary dealer statistics, and market stress signals
- LIQUIDITY_COMPOSITE_INDEX.md: Three-pillar theoretical framework, Z-score
  normalization, weighting rationale, and practical applications

All documentation follows narrative style with economic reasoning, avoiding
bullet-heavy lists in favor of flowing explanatory prose.

Settlement Fails Integration:
- Added nyfed_settlement_fails.py: Fetches 22 Treasury fails series across
  all maturities (2Y, 3Y, 5Y, 7Y, 10Y, 20Y, 30Y, FRN, TIPS)
- Discovered and integrated NY Fed Primary Dealer Statistics API endpoints
- Aggregates Fails to Deliver + Fails to Receive into total fails metric
- Calculates moving averages (MA5, MA20) and Z-scores for stress detection
- Complete historical data from 2022-01-05 to present (202+ weeks)
- Full documentation in SETTLEMENT_FAILS_SUCCESS.md with endpoint discovery

Code Improvements:
- nyfed_operations.py: Added submission_ratio calculation (demand/capacity)
  for repo stress monitoring, fixed data aggregation to handle multiple
  operations per day correctly (numeric sum, string first)
- liquidity_composite_index.py: Added duplicate date handling for all data
  sources, flexible column matching (Total_Taxes fallback)
- api_client.py: Implemented fetch_settlement_fails() method with 22-series
  aggregation, handles suppressed data (*) gracefully

README Update:
- Complete project overview with three-pillar structure clearly explained
- Installation and quick start instructions
- Links to all comprehensive documentation
- LCI interpretation guide with regime classification
- Updated contact information and license

System Status:
âœ… Fiscal Analysis: Fully operational
âœ… Fed Liquidity Monitor: Fully operational
âœ… NY Fed Operations: Fixed and enhanced
âœ… Settlement Fails: Newly integrated and operational
âœ… Liquidity Composite Index: Complete with all components

The LCI now provides complete market liquidity assessment with:
- Fiscal Liquidity (40%): Government cash flows
- Monetary Liquidity (35%): Fed balance sheet operations
- Market Plumbing (25%): Repo stress (60%) + Settlement fails (40%)

Total additions: ~12,600 words of documentation, 173-line settlement fails
fetcher, critical bug fixes, and enhanced system robustness.

Subject: docs: enhance analysis framework with comprehensive desk-grade template
Message Body:
This commit establishes a production-ready analysis framework for integrated
Fed liquidity and fiscal impulse monitoring, following institutional desk
methodology.

## Changes

### 1. Enhanced Analysis Specification (fiscal/prompt_analysis.md)
- Expanded from basic requirements to comprehensive 8-section template
- Added mandatory structure: Executive Summary â†’ 8 analytical sections â†’ Conclusion
- Included detailed formatting requirements (Unicode tables, status symbols)
- Specified tone & style guidelines (professional desk-grade language)
- Added pre-publication checklist for quality assurance
- Integrated Fed liquidity metrics with fiscal data for holistic view

Key additions:
- Section 0: Executive Summary with key findings
- Section 1: Fiscal Impulse Analysis (vs 0.64% GDP target)
- Section 2: Time-Frame Decomposition (MTD/QTD/FYTD)
- Section 3: Historical Comparison (YoY, 3Y baseline)
- Section 4: Liquidity Composition (TGA, Household Absorption)
- Section 5: Fed Liquidity & Monetary Conditions
- Section 6: Integrated Liquidity View (fiscal + monetary)
- Section 7: Risk Assessment & Outlook
- Section 8: Actionable Intelligence (rates/equities/macro)

### 2. Analysis Output (fed-treasury/docs/daily_analysis_2025-11-25.md)
- Added comprehensive Nov 25, 2025 analysis following new template
- Documents current regime: "Stealth Easing" (fiscal dominance despite QT)
- Key findings:
  * Fiscal impulse 0.51% GDP (-21% vs target)
  * RRP near depletion ($1B, -98% MTD) - critical threshold
  * Net liquidity rising +$53B MTD despite QT
  * FYTD spending +$92B (+8.9% YoY)

### 3. Minor Fix (fed/fed_liquidity.py)
- Fixed string formatting syntax (curly braces in f-string)

## Impact

This framework enables:
- Consistent, reproducible desk-grade analysis
- Integration of Treasury fiscal flows with Fed monetary operations
- Actionable intelligence for rates, equity, and macro positioning
- Early warning system for liquidity stress (RRP depletion, reserve adequacy)

## Methodology

Replicates Primary Dealer "Fiscal Week" methodology with enhancements:
- Daily Treasury Statement (DTS) parsing (Tables I & II)
- Fed H.4.1 balance sheet data integration
- Net Liquidity calculation: Fed Assets - RRP - TGA
- GDP-normalized fiscal impulse (target: 0.64% weekly)
- Stress index composite (SOFR spreads, RRP usage, volatility)
